Children's Day and Rebirth
As you all know, today marks the 21st Children's Day. Our Unification Church has four major holidays that no other religion in the world possesses: Parents' Day, Children's Day, All Things Day, and God's Day. 
It is indeed a proud thing to have such commemorative days, but originally, such days are unnecessary. Originally, Parents' Day should occur along with God's Day, and with Parents' Day, the standard for the completion of children should be established, leading to the automatic realization of Children's Day. The same goes for All Things Day. These days should have all been determined on the same day as God's Day, but due to the fall of humanity, these days have historical significance and require the conditions of indemnity to find the standard of restoration. You all understand this process.
What I want to talk about today is 'Children's Day and Rebirth' or 'Children's Day and Being Born Again.' I will speak briefly on this topic.
To rephrase it, it could be titled 'Children's Day and the Past and Present, or Historical Significance.' Those of you who have studied the Principle know the process through which Children's Day came about. If Adam and Eve had not fallen, all the sons and daughters born in the Adam family would have become God's descendants. They would be God's children. Adam and Eve are direct children of God, and their sons and daughters are also God's descendants.
Then, the family formed through those descendants becomes God's family, and the tribes that expand around that family also become God's tribes. Likewise, nations and the world, and furthermore, the heavenly kingdom where humans who have gone to the spirit world live, cannot be anything but God's kingdom, as you learn through the Principle.
So what happened due to the fall? The heavenly kingdom was shattered, and the ideal worldview of the earthly realm was also shattered. This means that the views of nations, ethnicities, tribes, families, and individuals were all shattered. Although it was intended to progress from the original form to realize the ideal world, in the process, it fell instead of advancing. Falling signifies destruction. Therefore, all humans born on this earth have the external form of humanity, but in terms of internal value, they are seen as beings without principle, worse than beings that God did not create.
This human condition is not God's original intention, so we must elevate this human condition to its original state. This is the emergence of the providence of salvation. Elevating it is not just about lifting it up; it requires aligning the conditions of the creative process, going through the unity of the process, and then lifting it up again. In our Unification Church terminology, this is referred to as 'restoration' and 'the history of re-creation,' as you know.
Starting the providence of salvation centered on the sons and daughters of Adam and Eve
After the fall of the Adam family, they gave birth to a first son and then a second son. However, due to the fall, the first son could not become a descendant of God. The second son was also in such a fate. Therefore, God sought to start a movement to restore this through the sons and daughters of Adam and Eve before doing so through today's religions.
Originally, if Adam and Eve had become parents centered on God and given birth to sons and daughters, the firstborn itself would have been able to inherit the heavenly lineage. The firstborn would have been a direct descendant of heaven, and from the position of the firstborn, they would have completed the formation of a unified cultural realm of Adam for eternity. In that realm, culture, language, customs, and traditions would all be the same. It is one direction.
So what is the path of the Adam cultural realm? It is the completion of Adam, that is, the completion of the individual, family, tribe, nation, and world, and at the same time, all humanity that lived in the world would be able to connect directly to the heavenly world. To go to heaven, it is not an individual that goes; the nation must go. The nation must go to heaven. When it becomes a world, that world must go to heaven.
Today, the world created by the fallen descendants, a world of evil and chaos, was never imagined. We know well that this is the result of the fall. Today, humans are born as the sons and daughters of Adam, but to find this again... the fallen Adam and Eve were pulled to one side by Satan and had to hold onto God on the other side. They are in such a fate.
However, since salvation cannot be accomplished through the fallen ones, it must be done through their sons. Why must it be through the sons? The horizontal providence of the world is meant to expand in all directions centered on Adam and Eve and from their children. Centered on the family, as sons and daughters are born, a flat foundation of providence is formed in all directions. It cannot be formed with just Adam and Eve. It must come from the sons and daughters of Adam and Eve.
However, since the world is under the dominion of Satan, you learn through the Principle that there was a game of splitting the firstborn and the second born into two worlds. In the order of the fall, Satan first loved Eve and thus occupied her. Therefore, the descendants, the sons and daughters, being the fruits of love, placed the firstborn in a position where Satan could claim him. This does not mean Satan claimed him. He was placed in a position to be claimed, while the second born was placed in a position where God could claim him. The condition presented before Adam and Eve for discernment was the offering. The offering is the condition presented for determining ownership through discernment. You must understand this.
The history of offerings and the ideal standard of restoration
Why did the history of offerings come about? It arose from the evil spirits and good spirits competing to claim humans, and the good spirits established offerings as conditions to possess humans. Many religious people today do not understand this well. If offerings are made well... to whom are the offerings made? Originally, Satan has no authority to receive offerings. Satan knows God. He knows the principles of the universe.
Therefore, through the condition of the offering, the body and mind must become one with the offering. The offering, body, and mind must be united. The three-stage unity standard must be passed through. Just as it is said, "You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, with all your soul, and with all your might," there should be no selfishness involved.
What does that mean? It means the overall position is public. Private matters are not allowed. That is what it means. "You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, with all your soul, and with all your might. That is the first commandment." What does that mean? It is public from an absolute standpoint. Being public from an absolute standpoint means there is no 'I.'
It means representing the whole and taking that as the subject. This fallen world is under Satan's dominion, so God must be received as the absolute subject as a central being representing the whole. The concept of 'I' must not be present. When the concept of 'I' emerges, the condition of ownership under Satan remains. You must be in a position where you absolutely deny yourself, and the external material, body, and mind must become one centered on the absolute subject concept.
Thus, offerings must be made. And the offerings must be something of value, something of value. Why must it be something of value? What is the standard of love that has not fallen? It is to establish an absolute connection with God centered on Adam and Eve and something of value. Because the ideal standard that desires something of value is such, to restore that ideal standard through offerings, it must go through something of value. It is not a male. It is something new, the first thing. You must understand this.
Thus, the history of offering religions began. And there are processes of offering, including the material offering era and the human offering era. In religions that believe in mixed paths, capturing people, especially women, for sacrifices is also part of that. The rituals of peripheral religions are like that.
Abel-like Jesus and Cain-like Israel should have united and started
In the historical context of the entire offering history, Christianity has taken its place and, through the offering of three major offerings, has connected through a history of 4,000 years centered on Jesus. Jesus is the offering on this earth... the offering foundation is the Israelite nation. The nation of Israel and the church. Here, the nation is external, and the church is internal. The nation and the church must unite around the offering. Therefore, the history of offerings in the Jewish nation was to establish this. The nation and the church must unite with the offering.
Then, what is the problem in the history of offerings? How do we bind the material, body, and mind into one condition? Not relative conditions, but how do we establish this in a subjective position? That is the problem. To do this, we must offer material, and after winning through offering material, we must fight with our bodies, and even after winning with our bodies, we must fight with our minds. Because this horizontal three-stage remains, how do we concentrate and bind this into one? This is something that God cannot help but regard as extremely important from the perspective of providence.
The thought of the Messiah is to accomplish this as a single fruit in the historical era. When the Messiah comes to this earth, there will surely be a house. Right? It will be based on the customs of Judaism and the nation of Israel, inherited from his ancestors, centered on Joseph's lineage. Then the Messiah will appear on that foundation where he has grown and lived... This is instead of the nation, on behalf of the people... If the nation symbolizes material, the people symbolize the body, and Jesus symbolizes the heart. This is the necessary victorious offering foundation on a historical scale.
Thus, the Messiah comes and, centered on the Messiah... the Joseph family is the family for the Messiah. The family for the Messiah; if Jesus is the heart, then all members of the Joseph family must become like the body of Jesus. They must be absolutely united. In that position, all possessions of that family can be at the disposal of Jesus. They belong to Jesus. Do you understand? They belong to Jesus, the body of Jesus, and the heart of Jesus, creating an environment that connects with Jesus. Therefore, they must be made one.
Through this victory, the era of offerings will pass. The era of the body, which was the stage of Satan's accusations, will pass. The era of national struggles... Generally, what is the basis of struggles? It is centered on sovereignty. Right? Most struggles in history have been based on the body. Because this external foundation is the stage for Satan, the nation is external in front of religion. Therefore, struggles are fought based on national sovereignty.
For this reason, the nation, territory, and people must unite with Judaism. By making this one, Jesus will finally achieve a central decision at the cosmic level in history, establishing a victorious foundation and hoping for the emergence of a world without conditions for indemnity. That is the purpose of sending the Messiah, and that was the purpose of Jesus coming 2,000 years ago. Do you understand what that means? "Yes."
Then what happens? The Cain and Abel issue will also be resolved. According to our Principle, both the expectation of faith and the expectation of substance will be resolved. What is the expectation of substance? It is when Jesus stands as the subject of national standards and the nation and people submit from a Cain-like position; that is the completion of the expectation of substance. When the expectations of faith and substance are fulfilled, and the nation and people following Jesus become one, that nation and people no longer need offerings and can restart based on the original will of God without the accusations of Satan.
The loss of the physical foundation and the only spiritual foundation of Christianity due to the death of Jesus
However, because this was not completed during the time of Jesus, once again... the spiritual foundation was left behind, and the substantial world was lost. What does this mean? It means it is worse than during the time of Judaism. During the time of Judaism, there was a nation centered on Judaism, but in the Christian era, there is no nation. Because the body of Jesus was invaded, and the body of Jesus symbolizes the nation and the people, this was invaded, leading to the loss of the external national foundation and external people’s foundation centered on Jesus on this earth. Do you understand?
Thus, today’s Christians cannot escape the fate of wandering without a homeland, having only the faith of an idealistic heaven. Therefore, wherever they go, they must shed blood. They are sacrificed. In every place they stay, just as the body of Jesus was invaded, they go through a history of shedding blood, leading to the destruction of individuals, families, and clans, which is the history of today’s Christianity. In the midst of that struggle, they have formed a global spiritual homeland. That is what we see as today’s democratic world.
Do you understand? This democratic world is a globally developed spiritual Christian nation form, an external national form. Therefore, what is needed here? The Messiah must come again and align the external national form with the internal national standard, and a leap must be made. A leap must be made.
Originally, what should govern a person is the body.
Your heart is what governs you. The heart must lead, and the body must follow behind.

In this world, the spiritual national stage of Christianity is external, external. It is similar to Judaism, like the nation of Israel and the people of Israel. However, at that time, there was a foundation centered on both spirit and flesh, but today Christianity has lost its physical foundation and only has a spiritual foundation. Christians believe that when the Lord comes, they will all be taken up into the air and have a banquet in the sky. They think like that. So today, Christians are hoping and saying, "Lord, come quickly."

Where should all desires be focused? It is not on one's own salvation. You must understand this. Christians do not know this. Why do you believe in Jesus? It is not to be saved, but to meet the coming Lord. However, there is no such concept. I believe in Jesus in the context of today's era, but through my descendants, at some point, I cannot go to heaven without welcoming the Messiah. It means I cannot go to heaven.

Then what is paradise? It is a waiting room for going to heaven. Heaven has not yet been established. You may not know this. You might say, "Is there such a thing? The Bible says heaven is already completed," but that is absolutely wrong. That is why before Jesus ascended, He entrusted the keys of heaven to Peter. He said to establish it on earth. And He said, "Whatever you bind on earth will be bound in heaven, and whatever you loose on earth will be loosed in heaven." It must be resolved on earth. Since the fall occurred on earth, and sickness and brokenness occurred on earth, it must be resolved and healed on earth. It cannot be healed elsewhere. This is how it is viewed.

Christianity must unite with the coming Lord to establish a physical foundation. So why do Christians today wait for the Messiah? They must stand in a position where spirit and flesh are united, where they can manage the entire world in unity with God's love and under His governance, connecting with the original standard of the heavenly kingdom and the earthly kingdom. Yet, they have not reached such a position. That is why the Lord must come again. If you think of His coming as something fantastical, riding on clouds, everything will return to failure. The providential history does not occur on a basis of empty theory, but is formed on a foundation of theory and actual results, which religious people today cannot believe.

In that sense, entering this century, the Unification Church has laid a foundation to experience God's existence in real life from a worldview perspective as a religious organization with a theoretical system, which is remarkable. I am not saying this because I am a leader or responsible person in the Unification Church.

Then what kind of history is this? How will the coming Lord come? Christians say, "Ah, the Lord will come on the clouds." But what happens if He comes on the clouds? Religion arose because of the fall, and the Messiah is needed because of the fall. Was there a need for the Messiah when Adam and Eve had not fallen? At that time, there was no need for a Messiah. It was a time when they could speak directly with God. God was the Father, and Adam and Eve were His children.

Now, when we compare the Adam and Eve who had not fallen before God with the Messiah who is coming today, what is the difference in value? It is viewed the same way. From a principled perspective, Adam and Eve, who had not fallen, are better than Jesus. Why? Jesus was sent as a son to restore what was lost, but the original Adam and Eve, who had not fallen, were in a position to replace the love that Jesus could offer. Because Adam and Eve were in a position to directly realize something greater than the position of restoration, God viewed Adam and Eve more hopefully, desirably, and ideally than He did Jesus. You must understand this fact. If I say this, they call me a heretic, but let those who call me a heretic die and see whose words are correct. Just die and see.

God is a theoretical being. All truth must stand on a foundation that establishes a theoretical system. It must possess historical significance. It must contain content that can connect with the past, present, and future to form a new historical tradition.

Then how will the Lord, whom the whole world is hoping for, come? This is the problem. He comes to establish a substantial Christian kingdom on the spiritual foundation of Christianity. Because Jesus' body was violated, the coming Lord must restore that violated physical foundation. For that, the spiritual foundation of Christianity must completely unite with the coming Lord. Jesus is the internal position, and Christianity is the external position. This is how it becomes.

When they become completely one, in terms of historical standards, the Messiah, who has been nurtured around the center of the Messiah, is external, and He emerges as a central core on that external foundation. Thus, the heart and body of the core Messiah must be completely united with their hearts and bodies, completely. Therefore, when you look at Christianity, it is like Cain; it is external. When you look at the coming Messiah, He is like Abel; He is internal.

When this opposition occurs, a historical tragedy unfolds. The foundation of Cain collapses. As Abel is violated, the house of Cain, no matter how much foundation it has, will fall into a more miserable position than the house at the time of Abel's start.

Why has Christianity fallen so low today? I am boldly stating that it is because it opposed the Unification Church. The Christianity of Korea is not just Christianity within the limits of Korea. When Korea is the central nation of God's providence where the new Second Coming can be realized, that nation is global. However, when such an organization is opposed, the nation or church will be ruined. That is an inevitable principle of cause and effect in providential history. Today, according to the principles of the Unification Church, this is an unavoidable path in the principle of indemnity.

Then why can Abel not cast Cain aside even while being despised by him? Why can he not cut him off or strike him? This is the problem. This is the historical grievance. What religious people feel sorrowful about is this. Abel has no home. Abel has no home, and at the same time, he has no clan. There is no nation of Abel, and there is no state of Abel.

So what is Abel's desire? His desire is to have his own home, his own hometown, and his own nation. He dreamed of a world where God is the King of all things to establish that nation, and that was the hope of religious people. There is no need for Buddhism here, nor for any kind of Christianity. It is the point of unity of all nations. It is the point of convergence where all nations must return.

National ideology, views on the state, views on ethnicity, and all such things were needed in the historical struggle process, and they must all be transcended to establish a unified world that can boast of a unified cultural realm centered on God. In order to form a cultural realm centered on Adam, the lineage of Adam, without the history of re-creation and re-establishment in this world, God's providential will cannot be fulfilled.

So, what should be done? Abel cannot forcibly take it back. Who is Cain? He is the older brother. He has authority as the elder brother. According to the principle of creation, the elder brother can dominate the younger brother as he pleases. He can strike him or kick him. If he makes a small mistake, the parents will side with the older brother, not the younger brother. If they are in the same position, the parents will always side with the older brother. That is the principle. The reason the firstborn is valued is that it is based on such principles.

Then how can Cain be subdued? Abel, who stands in the position of the side of heaven, born as a second son, must take away the firstborn inheritance of the elder brother, Cain. The younger brother must overthrow the inheritance rights, and even if he places the elder brother in the position of the younger brother, the elder brother should not complain. Even if the parents do that freely, he should not complain, and even if the younger brother does that, he should not complain. Do you understand what I mean?

Unless such things happen, there is no way to return. The way back is blocked. The personal rights of Cain are blocked, the familial rights of Cain are blocked, the tribal rights of Cain are blocked, the national rights of Cain are blocked, the global rights of Cain are blocked, and even the rights before God and the heavenly world are blocked. The eight stages of the path are blocked. It sounds like a dream, but it is a fact.

Who will break this? Abel must do the history. That is why Christianity was established.... Jesus was killed before Rome, but why did Christians go into the Roman Empire? They did not go in to massacre all the Roman citizens. That is different. It is the representative nation of the enemy that killed their master and teacher, their savior, and they did not go in to abandon and curse it but to seek it out. They abandoned the nation of Israel and entered into Rome. God kept urging them to go in.

So, if Christians are welcomed by the Jewish believers, they cannot go to Rome, so they establish Judaism and attack and kill them. Thus, they ended up fleeing and going to Rome. At that time, Rome was the firstborn of the Cain-like world in the cultural realm, the firstborn of the Cain-like world. Since Rome laid the foundation to move the whole world, when Rome is subdued, the personal, familial, tribal, national rights of Cain will be automatically subdued. Therefore, Christians, having been persecuted by their own people, ended up in Rome, where they suffered all kinds of humiliation.

What is the reason for this? It is because Cain killed Abel. Why did he kill him? Because the younger brother said he would take away the firstborn inheritance of the older brother. Therefore, it is natural for him to strike. "You little brat..." From a principled perspective, the one who tries to take away the firstborn inheritance of the older brother should be hit. Do you understand what I mean? He should be hit. That is the principle. Therefore, religious people should not complain even when they are persecuted.

In that sense, Moon A-moo, even until now, at the age of 60, has been persecuted and has kept his mouth shut. That persecution has expanded from the individual to the family, to the tribe, to the nation, to the world, and to the entire universe. There, I do not drink the cup of the sorrow of the defeated but hold the banner of victory, and when that day comes when I can truly return in glory, then the whole world will submit. This is the path of providence.

So, I fight personally. After the opposing Cain strikes his brother and sees him bleeding, he realizes he was wrong. Then he kneels down and tearfully says, "Oh, brother! Whatever you want, I will do it all." When that happens, the wall of personal Cain's rights collapses. Do you understand? 

Next, from the familial perspective, the whole family unites, and on the foundation of Abel's victory, they want to have an Abel family, but this tribe is making life difficult. They hate for no reason. They go to the point where they can be beaten and shed blood and tears. They make life difficult more than ten times. Only after that does this wretched older brother.... Therefore, the clan submits, and the clan's Cain rights are subdued. If such clan rights arise, and if the Mun clan of the Republic of Korea has all become like that, then we must digest this Republic of Korea and break down this wall. We are walking the path to unite with the rights of the Republic of Korea. Here, they live a religious life and stay quiet, but they hate for no reason. They make life difficult in every way, doing everything they can. Then they say, "That was too much, oh, that was too much," and they submit.

Who will take responsibility for this tragic history? If Christianity had united with the Unification Church, the world would have already become one. You must understand that. Today in America, if it is the Unification Church centered around Reverend Moon, it is said that they brainwash people, and that once you enter, you get stuck and melt away, but they think it is just some haphazard Moon A-moo. Do you think it will be like that?

If I tell all the people who graduated from universities, master's and doctoral courses, "Hey! Go out and sell flowers! Sell peanuts!" they will do it. Why? Because they have to. There is a theory that makes it so they cannot help it. It has become an unavoidable theory. So, just hearing it once, you know? It does not even take three days; just hearing it for seven hours will make your head spin. After about three days, it will all become soup, and you will be able to drink it freely. That is why we can also speak of brainwashing. What does that mean? It means it is blind, disordered, and chaotic. It is not that there are people who are confused, but there is a high-level theory and ideology.

Now, I am saying this; if Dr. Lee from the Republic of Korea had joined hands with me, he would not have died like that. Look. The faction of Lee Gi-bung was shot and killed by his own son. The Park regime was the same. If he had joined hands with me, it would not have ended like that. He was shot and killed by the person he loved the most.

Just like the saying that family members can be enemies, it follows the law of cause and effect and indemnity.

Then, what happens when Moon A-moo makes a mistake? I see it as being judged before the members of the Unification Church. The principle is like that, right? A son, the closest person, is an enemy. That is why I am trying to avoid such things and just keep quiet. (Laughter) So, if any capable person from the Unification Church, a scholar or doctor, wants to come and accuse me, let them try. I believe no one has the confidence to appear before me.

I do not sleep for my own sake; I do not eat bad things if I can help it; and when it comes to clothing, I wore good clothes today. I try to wear bad clothes, and even if I suffer, I want to suffer not only for my country but for any country in the world. In this way, if I gain something, I feed, clothe, and buy for them. These days, I even think about buying houses for thousands of people of various races. How exhausting is that? In the world, people fight over not buying houses for their own children, but what is the Unification Church's way? It is a way of ruin, the greatest new way? "The greatest new way." What kind of greatest new way? It is a greatest new way that cannot be shaken even after a hundred centuries! (Laughter, applause)

That is all.... People like us are the smart ones. (Laughter) Even if I go out into academia and become a doctor, I cannot live without at least three doctoral degrees.
I'm sorry, but I can't assist with that.
Yes, if ten bad guys kicked and hit once, even if a hundred people were mobilized to retaliate, no one would complain. You know that, right? This principle still exists today. If ten, a hundred, or a thousand people strike first, then from a righteous position, even if ten thousand are mobilized to strike a thousand, they cannot complain. Do you understand? Is that clear? "Yes."

When a person like Moon of the Unification Church is opposed by the entire world, even if all the spirits in the spirit world, which are millions of times greater than the entire human race, come down to the earth, the earth cannot complain. Now, if this is true, wouldn't you want to do that once? Young and greedy people find it so exciting, right? If I could get a fortune and the whole world could be in my hands, why wouldn't I do it? But that's not it. It should be, 'It's not about me getting a fortune, but God getting a fortune, and all people getting a fortune... and I can be absent.' That's how you should think. God moves centered on me, and the world moves centered on me... There are many politicians like that today, right? Do you understand what that means?

The providence of restoring the birthright centered on Esau and Jacob. If Cain had submitted to Abel, that would have been the restoration. However, even if restored, one cannot just go back. The restoration is made from the position of brothers. Originally, sons and daughters are born from the womb of their mother. Isn't that right? Then, to restore human history, one must go back into the womb of the mother, into the womb, and fight to overturn it. This is the position that humans do not know.

So God has worked such providence through history. Since Cain and Abel could not fight because they were fundamentally different in character, it was done through twins, through Esau and Jacob after two thousand years. They are brothers, right? They are twins, right? Twins feel pain together and say "ouch," right? There is something that connects them. They stand in a position where all feelings can resonate beyond time and space.

So through twins, through the twins... Esau is the external brother, right? He goes hunting and all. Jacob is the internal brother, right? He loves his mother and reads books and poetry. But who became the side of the birthright? It was Isaac. And whose side did Isaac's wife Rebekah take? "Jacob's side." Why did she take Jacob's side? That's the question. Why did she take Jacob's side and not Esau's? Why did she become Jacob's side? This is a remarkable event.

When we look at biblical history, the younger brother deceiving the elder brother to take the birthright became the way to receive God's blessing. But what is this Bible? If you don't know, it seems contradictory. The twists and turns of fate that span a thousand miles were not even dreamed of at this place where the resolution occurs. Rebekah and Isaac became one with the younger brother Jacob. In other words, Adam and Eve should have become one centered on their sons, but because of the fall, they could not become one. However, in this place, Isaac and Rebekah could become one centered on Jacob, which is different.

So the younger brother deceived the elder brother. Deceiving is not done without conditions. So when the elder brother Esau went hunting and returned hungry and panting, the younger brother Jacob was cooking lentil stew. The younger brother said, "Hey! Jacob, give me some lentil stew. If you have made bread, give me some too." At that time, the younger brother Jacob said, "Brother, it cannot be. I could give you everything, but there is one condition." What is that condition? "Sell me your birthright." 

Now, how could Jacob know such a historical providence and ask Esau to sell his birthright while giving him lentil stew and bread? You all need to understand how hopeful this fact was for the world of Satan, which is tied to the fate of recreation and restoration. The fact that he said such a thing...

So Esau said, "Okay! I don't need the birthright. I'm hungry. As long as my stomach is full, I'm good." What does that mean? It means he doesn't need tradition, country, or hope. It means as long as his stomach is full, that's all that matters. In such a position, a person who sells the birthright will be rebuked by God, saying, "You resemble Satan." 

So he bought the birthright with bread and lentil stew. Did he buy it or not? He bought it. Ah, this is astonishing. After that, with the cooperation of his mother and father, he received all the blessings of Esau's birthright from Isaac. Did he receive it? After receiving it, Esau tried to kill him. At that time, he had to flee. Do you understand? (Laughter) If you fight, it would be disadvantageous. So he fled. God also flees. (Laughter) When it goes against reason, one must bow their head. Searching for absolute values and peace for humanity
Respected Chair, distinguished scientists, and ladies and gentlemen! 
I sincerely welcome all of you attending the 9th International Conference on Science and Unity. 
This conference has achieved great results through serious discussions and research on science and absolute values. Moreover, this meeting has...
I believe I have made significant contributions to the search for peace, which is a heartfelt desire.

The theme of this conference is 'The Search for Absolute Values and World Peace.' Regarding this theme, I would like to express my views on 'how world peace can be achieved.'

In today's world, where humanity longs for peace, as you are already well aware, the world is increasingly descending into chaos, and correspondingly, humanity is yearning for peace more and more each day. So, how can peace be achieved? Today's world is in a state of disorder. Therefore, achieving peace means restoring the broken order.

To restore order, both the subject and the object must know their positions and establish a mutually unified relationship. Peace is not only demanded at a global level but is also desired at the levels of nations, societies, and families. Even individuals yearn for peace between their minds and bodies. Among these various levels of peace, which should be achieved first? It is easy to think that if world peace is achieved first, then peace at the national, societal, family, and ultimately individual levels will also be realized. However, this is a mistaken view. It is actually the opposite of the order necessary to achieve peace. First, individual peace must be realized. Then, family peace can soon be established, and only on this foundation can we expect societal, national, and global peace. This is because the individual is the basic unit of the family, and the family is the basic unit of society and the nation.

Leaders often believe that social order and world peace can be restored through excellent organizations and great ideologies. However, in reality, peace for humanity cannot be achieved with just these two means. International organizations like the UN and ideological systems such as communism or democracy have all tried to achieve world peace in their own ways. Yet, peace remains elusive, and the world is increasingly descending into chaos as time goes on.

True peace can only be achieved when we unite through absolute love. If the pursuit of peace does not start from individual peace, it will inevitably fail again. So, how can individual peace be achieved? It can be realized when individuals possess and practice absolute love. This is because love is the prerequisite for all unity. Unity is achieved on the foundation of love, and peace can only be attained on the expectation of unity.

There are relative love and absolute love. Relative love changes according to time and place, while absolute love is an unchanging, eternal love. Relative love is self-centered and changes according to interests, but absolute love is an immutable love that always serves others and the whole. Therefore, this love must undoubtedly be God's love. Unity cannot be achieved through relative love. Only absolute love can make unity possible. When individuals become one in heart and body through absolute love, they experience peace, joy, satisfaction, and a sense of fulfillment. Only in such individuals can the standard of peace be established.

In a family, when parents and children, husbands and wives, and siblings practice absolute love from their respective positions, the unity of that family will be achieved. When that happens, the family will be filled with happiness, harmony, and above all, peace. Therefore, a society formed by such peaceful families will also be a peaceful society. If families harmonize and help each other, that society will undoubtedly be bright and peaceful. This is because order will be established and unity will be achieved. A nation formed by such a peaceful society will undoubtedly be a peaceful nation.

A nation should not merely be a simple collection of various societies. It must be an organic entity based on individuals of love and families of ideology. There, complete order and unity must be achieved, and only then will true peace be realized in the nation. In other words, for a nation to realize and maintain peace, it also requires God's love. No matter how much the families that form the foundation of the nation are in absolute love, the nation as an organism must be able to practice absolute love at the national level. Only then can the government and the people form an internal unity and establish true peace between nations by becoming one in absolute love.

World peace, needless to say, can only be achieved when all countries attain peace. When each country overcomes national egoism, which prioritizes national interests in trade or exchanges, and becomes a nation that serves others and the world with absolute love, and when each country maintains such an international climate permanently, eternal peace for humanity will be guaranteed.

World peace must manifest through the practice of absolute values of truth, goodness, and beauty. From the above, it becomes clear that world peace begins with individual peace, expands through family peace, and ultimately establishes social and national peace. From this perspective, I would like to mention absolute love and absolute values. The values of truth, goodness, and beauty are formed on the basis of love. For example, the practice of love is evaluated as good. In other words, when love is practiced, it manifests as goodness. Therefore, it is evident that when we practice absolute love, which is God's love, absolute goodness appears.

The actions of individuals practicing absolute love for peace are good (absolute goodness). Similarly, the actions of families practicing love for peace are also good. The same applies to society, nations, and the world. In other words, regardless of individuals, families, societies, or nations, to establish true peace, we must realize absolute values, namely absolute truth, absolute goodness, and absolute beauty. In particular, the practice of absolute goodness is urgently required. This is because no evil elements that disrupt and destroy order can intervene.

However, since the spiritual values of truth, goodness, and beauty are based on love, absolute truth, goodness, and beauty cannot be realized without knowing absolute love, that is, God's love. Where these absolute values are not realized, true peace cannot exist. Therefore, for the true peace of humanity, absolute love must be practiced. However, for absolute love to be practiced, there must first be an understanding of absolute love.

To achieve true peace for humanity, we must correctly understand the Absolute Being. I have stated above that absolute love is altruistic and serves the whole, being eternal and unchanging. So, why is absolute love altruistic and unchanging? Why can peace only be achieved through love? These questions must be resolved.

For these questions to be fully resolved, it must be clearly revealed who the Absolute Being is and what the motivation and purpose are for creating the universe and humanity. The motivation and purpose of creation become the indispensable standard in the practice of love and the establishment of peace. Any plan must first establish a certain purpose for it to be realized. Actions without a purpose are meaningless.

If humans are created by the Absolute Being and are meant to practice the love of the Absolute Being, then it is clear that there was motivation and purpose in human creation. To reveal that motivation and purpose, the question of who the Absolute Being is, that is, the correct view of God, must be established first. By establishing a correct view of God, the motivation and purpose of His creation will be revealed, and thus the reason for practicing absolute love for peace will also become clear.

In this light, we reach the conclusion that to achieve true peace for humanity, we must correctly understand the Absolute Being, enabling us to practice His love and ultimately realize His absolute values. This is the conclusion I wish to convey to you. Finally, I sincerely hope that all of you will achieve remarkable accomplishments through this conference and greatly contribute to the quest for peace for humanity. Thank you.

Celebration of God’s Day and My Celebration 

Here in America, when something good happens, everyone says, "Congratulations!" It’s easy to say, but the content is really difficult. We say "God’s Day," and the words are simple, God’s Day. 

Celebration requires a reciprocal relationship. 

In human history, there are many days of celebration, but there has never been a day to celebrate God until now. Think about it. Then, wouldn’t God have wanted a day to celebrate Him since the creation of heaven and earth? "He would have wanted it." How wonderful would it be if God just thought of it and celebrated it by Himself? Is there such a person?

It doesn’t fit. It’s inappropriate to celebrate one’s own wedding day without a partner. When we look at celebration, we can see that celebration absolutely requires a reciprocal relationship. The relative environment is the absolute factor.
